  </td>
 </tr>

  <td width="55%" valign="top" style="padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:55.14%;">
  <p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:2.94%;">

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in .6in .0001pt 0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(All
amounts expressed in U.S. dollars unless otherwise noted)</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AGNICO-EAGLE PROVIDES
EXPLORATION UPDATE ON 2008 ACTIVITIES</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Toronto (March&nbsp;4,
2009) - <b>Agnico-Eagle Mines Limited</b>
(&#147;Agnico-Eagle&#148; or the &#147;Company&#148;) is pleased to provide an update on its 2008
exploration program.&#160; During 2008, the
Company spent approximately $72 million on exploration, including $38 million
of exploration capitalized at its development projects.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Exploration during 2008
resulted in a significant increase to the Company&#146;s overall reserves and
resources.&#160; See the following section
titled &#147;Detailed Mineral Reserve and Resource Data&#148; for the full details of the
Company&#146;s 2008 reserve and resource position.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Highlights of the 2008 Exploration Program Include:</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Symbol" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">8% increase in gold reserves to
a record level of 18.1 million ounces</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Symbol" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">13% increase in the indicated
gold resource to 3.2 million ounces</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Symbol" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">21% increase in the inferred
gold resource to 5.8 million ounces</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Symbol" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">At Meadowbank, mineralized
zones extended at depth, and along strike, at Goose South and Vault</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Symbol" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">At Pinos Altos, new gold-silver
reserves at San Eligio and Creston Mascota zones total 0.5 million ounces of
gold and 8.9 million ounces of silver</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Symbol" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Kittila adds more than 1.3
million ounces of inferred gold resource at depth on Suuri and Roura<b><i style="font-weight:bold;">  </i></b>zones</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 45.0pt;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;In 2008, we moved
steadily towards our goal of 20 million ounces of gold reserves from our
existing projects with the addition of 1.4 million ounces of reserves and 1.4
million ounces of resources&#148; said Sean Boyd, Vice-Chairman and CEO.&#160; &#147;With improving drill access at several of
our deposits, we expect to reach 20 million to 21 million ounces of gold
reserves by year end 2010.&#160; The ongoing
growth in our reserves is driving our scoping studies on four internal production
growth opportunities&#148; added Mr.&nbsp;Boyd.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">The Company&#146;s budgeted
exploration expenditure in 2009 is approximately $54 million and is expected to
result in total drilling of approximately 221 kilometres utilizing 25 drill
rigs.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Meadowbank
Exploration Update</font></u></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">At Meadowbank, the 2008 exploration campaign began in March&nbsp;with
a diamond drilling program followed by regional prospecting through early
September.&#160; Overall, 85 drill holes were
completed for a total of 24,028 metres.&#160;
Most of the drilling took place near the current resource envelopes at
Portage, Goose Island and Goose South and on other targets on the large
Meadowbank property, outside of the area of the mining licence.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/Mar09_MeadowbankGeologyMap.pdf</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A scoping study is
underway to consider an increase in the production rate at Meadowbank from the
design rate of 8,500 tonnes per day to a target rate of 10,000 tonnes per
day.&#160; The study is considering a higher
production rate from the open pits, as well as a scenario where the pit
material is supplemented by underground ore from the Goose South deposit.&#160; Results of the scoping study are expected in
the third quarter of 2009.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Portage
Deposit Extends On Southern End</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On the Portage zone of the Meadowbank deposit,
over 29 drill holes were completed for a total of 5,451 metres in 2008.&#160; </font>The focus of the exploration program at Portage was to convert inferred
resource located inside, or near, the southern limit of the Portage Pit, and to
explore the potential for<b><i style="font-weight:bold;">  </i></b>extending
the Portage Pit to the south.&#160; In this
area, the Bay and Portage zones occur adjacent to each other.</p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">One
of the northernmost holes of the Portage exploration program, hole TP08-774 (Section&nbsp;5650N),
cut two intervals corresponding to the Portage zone, averaging 4.5 grams per
tonne (&#147;g/t&#148;) over 5.5 metres and 2.4 g/t over 6.0 metres, respectively.&#160; The thickness of each intersection in this
news release is considered to be true width, unless otherwise indicated.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Fifty
metres to the south, hole TP08-769 (Section&nbsp;5600N) returned several Bay
zone intersections, with the best averaging 11.8 g/t over 4.1 metres.&#160; On the same section, hole TP08-768
intersected a Portage zone interval grading 1.8 g/t over 4.1 metres. These
drill holes are highlighted on the vertical cross section shown in the
following link.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/Mar09_PortageandBayZoneCrossSection.pdf</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A
further 50 metres to the south, hole TP08-767 (Section&nbsp;5550N) also cut two
intervals of the Bay zone and returned 19.0 g/t over 4.3 metres and 5.2 g/t
over 6.5 metres.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Another
50 metres to the south on Section&nbsp;5500N, one of the most significant
results to date on the Bay zone structure came from drill hole TP08-785, which
intersected two separate lenses, grading 6.3 grams per tonne of gold over 4.7
metres and 5.6 g/t over 4.1 metres.&#160; The
same drill hole intersected the Portage zone as well, returning 13.9 g/t of
gold over 8.3 metres.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">These
results contributed to increasing the year-end gold reserves at Meadowbank by
5% or 0.2 million ounces.&#160; The Portage
and Bay zones remain open to the south at depth for approximately 375 metres
towards the Goose Island deposit.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2</font></p>

<div style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left"></div>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">* Cutting factors of 38
g/t and 145 g/t have been applied to these sample results</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Goose South Underground Potential
Increasing</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">On the Goose South zone, 36 drill holes were
completed in 2008 for a total of 14,328 metres, to test the<b><i style="font-weight:bold;">  </i></b>underground
extension of the Goose Island open pit deposit. </font>&#160;This program was planned to increase the
definition of the zone to a depth of 300 metres, and also to test its depth
potential from 300 metres to 600 metres.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In the upper portion,
drill hole G08-797 on Section&nbsp;4300N returned encouraging values, as it
intersected two intervals. The first, which was associated with significant
visible gold, returned 63.4 g/t over 3.0 metres (6.4 g/t cut to 60 g/t ), while
the second averaged 7.1 g/t over 3.8 metres.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In the deeper portion, at
approximately 375 metres below surface, drill hole G08-821 on Section&nbsp;4600N
returned 5.6 g/t of gold over 4.5 metres, including 7.7 g/t over 3.4
metres.&#160; In the same area, drill hole
G08-818 on Section&nbsp;4500N returned 7.9 g/t over 4.3 metres, including 12.0
g/t over 2.7 metres.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/Mar09_GooseIslandGooseSouthLongSection.pdf</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">3</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Based on these
encouraging results, the indicated gold resource at Goose South has increased
to approximately 0.4 million ounces in 2.9 million tonnes, grading 4.2
g/t.&#160; In light of the zone being open at
depth, an underground exploration program, including a ramp system, is being
evaluated to provide better access to this zone.</font></p>

  <p align="right" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">524.5</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="3%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:3.14%;">

  <td width="3%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:3.14%;">

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Regional Exploration at Meadowbank
Yielding Encouraging Results at Vault South</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">In addition to regional prospecting to follow up on
anomalies discovered in 2007, twenty drill holes, for a total of 4,442 metres,
were also completed in 2008 on different targets outside of the current resource
limits at Meadowbank.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">One of the most significant results occurred at
Vault South.&#160; Following the prospecting
discovery of a similar style of gold mineralization to Vault, one shallow drill
hole VLT08-273, 180 metres in length, was completed to test this new
structure.&#160; This new zone of
mineralization sits approximately one kilometre to the southeast of the
deposit.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This hole intersected 2.6 g/t of gold over a
4.1 metre thick interval at a shallow depth (27 metres to 31.1 metres from the
drill hole collar).&#160; This discovery opens
a new drilling area in the Vault deposit area and is typical and similar to
previous historical discoveries on the Meadowbank property.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">For 2009, $11 million is budgeted for exploration in
Meadowbank region in Nunavut, including an estimated 47,800 metres in diamond
drilling for resource to reserve conversion and discovery of new gold zones.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">4</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Pinos Altos Exploration
Update</font></u></b></p>

<p style="background:white;color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During</font> 2008, at Pinos Altos in Mexico, exploration crews focused on
converting resources to reserves on the Creston Mascota area and at the main
mine development area.&#160; In addition to
the successful conversion of approximately 0.4 million ounces of gold resources
to reserves, the program also confirmed new gold zones in areas identified
during previous prospecting campaigns.&#160;
Creston Mascota is roughly seven kilometres to the northwest of the main
Santo Nino deposit at Pinos Altos.</p>

<p style="background:white;color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/Mar09_PinosAltosClaimMap.pdf</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/Mar09_PinosAltosGeologyMap.pdf</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Good Results at Creston
Mascota on the Pinos Altos Property</font></b></p>

<p style="background:white;color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As
a result of exploration activities in 2008, the Company reported a new probable
reserve at Creston Mascota of 0.4 million ounces of gold and 3.7 million ounces
of silver from 6.7 million tonnes grading 1.7 g/t of gold and 17.1 g/t of
silver.</font></p>

<p style="background:white;color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Prospecting
and mapping programs carried out in 2008, and to date in 2009, have traced the
Creston Mascota mineralization further to the southwest of the original
deposit.&#160; A road and drill pads have been
built.&#160; Approximately 5,000 metres of
drilling in 2009 are planned to extend mineralization in this zone.</font></p>

<p style="background:white;color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A
feasibility study is expected to be released soon on the potential to add
incremental production from the Creston Mascota deposit.&#160; The study is considering a stand-alone heap
leach operation.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/Mar09_CrestonMascotaCrossSection.pdf</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">San Eligio Returns High Grade Intersections</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Drilling on the San
Eligio deposit (a zone roughly 600 metres to the north and parallel to the main
Santo Nino deposit at Pinos Altos) has shown the presence of a higher grade
core located less than 200 metres below the surface.&#160; The deposit has been traced for approximately
one kilometre east-west and is still open along strike and at depths below 300
metres.&#160; An initial reserve at San Eligio
was estimated in 2008, with probable open pit and underground reserves totaling
118,000 ounces of gold and 5.2 million ounces of silver from 1.4 million tonnes,
grading 2.6 g/t of gold and 115 g/t of silver.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/Mar09_SanEligioLongitudinalSection.pdf</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">At San Eligio, the
geological interpretations and the results obtained from deep and lateral
exploration drilling suggest that there is a high grade area in the Eastern
part of the deposit.&#160; Several drill holes
testing this area returned high grade gold intersections.&#160; Hole PA-08-318 on Section&nbsp;5300E returned
5.2 g/t of gold and 150.5 g/t of silver over 3.8 metres.&#160; Hole PA-08-325 on Section&nbsp;5500E returned
16.8 g/t of gold and 361.7 g/t of silver over 4.2 metres associated with</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5</font></p>

<div style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">significant visible gold
and silver, while hole PA-08-327, also on Section&nbsp;5500E, returned 8.8 g/t
of gold and 171.1 g/t of silver over 6.9 metres at approximately 200 metres
below surface.</font></p>

  <p align="right" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">229.1</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="1%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.04%;">
  <p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">One drill rig is
currently pursuing the extensions of the deposit, including delineating the
high-grade area. It is expected that this initial reserve will grow during 2009
as almost 18,700 metres of drilling are planned in minesite exploration in
2009.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Exploration results at
Creston Mascota and San Eligio contributed to the 1.1 million ounce increase in
gold reserves and 27 million ounce increase in silver reserves at Pinos Altos
(increases of 41% and 37% respectively).&#160;
Almost $11 million in exploration spending is budgeted in 2009, mainly
on the Pinos Altos region, including an estimated 38,700 metres of diamond
drilling.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Kittila
Exploration Update</font></u></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Exploration at the
Kittila mine in northern Finland in 2008 has increased proven and probable gold
reserves to 3.2 million ounces (21.4 million tonnes grading 4.7 g/t) and more
than doubled the inferred gold resource to almost 2.5 million ounces (17.6
million tonnes grading 4.4 g/t), compared to 2007.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/Mar09_KittilaClaimMap.pdf</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">The increase in probable
reserves at Kittila is largely due to underground exploration success on the
Roura zone.&#160; This led to an increase in
year-end gold probable reserves at Roura of 150,000 ounces (a 27% increase to
0.7 million ounces in 5.1 million tonnes grading 4.4 g/t), as well as an
additional 190,000 ounces of inferred gold resource (a 19% increase compared to
year-end 2007 to almost 250,000 ounces in 2.6 million tonnes grading 3.0 g/t).
Underground ramp access has now reached both the Roura and the Suuri zones,
where exploration with two diamond drills in 2009 will begin to explore its
potential and better define known underground reserves, which currently extend
to a depth of 675 metres below surface.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">6</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/Mar09_KittilaLongitudinalSection.pdf</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Three Lenses Extend at Depth</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">The main Suuri zone is
made up of three roughly parallel lenses &#151; East, Central and West.&#160; Prior to 2008, resource exploration at depth
had focused on the East lens only.&#160;
During 2008, the potential of all three lenses had<b><i style="font-weight:bold;">  </i></b>begun
to be tested.&#160; Additional drills were
added which were capable of testing all three gold structures below the depths
of the current Suuri zone reserves and resources.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/Mar09_KittilaCrossSections.pdf</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Since September&nbsp;2008,
when the initial 1.0 million ounce inferred resource for the East lens was
announced, a new inferred resource has been discovered below the Suuri zone
reserves associated with the Central lens.&#160;
In addition, a new deep intercept on the Suuri zone&#146;s West lens suggests
that all three lenses may extend to depth.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Additional drilling at
depths up to 1,000 metres has continued to intersect the East Zone over a one
kilometre long strike length, north to south.&#160;
In holes SUU08005, SUU08006 and SUU08007 (see table below), multiple
medium to high grade gold intercepts have been cut over significant thicknesses
at depths of 800 metres or more, similar to results at the original Suuri
deposit.&#160; Accordingly, more deep
exploration at Suuri is planned for 2009.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">The discovery of the
Central lens resource has helped increase the Suuri inferred gold resource at
depth by 1.3 million ounces compared to year end 2007 to 2.0 million ounces in
12.7 million tonnes grading 4.8 g/t.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Since July&nbsp;2008,
when the possible depth extension of the Central lens was interpreted, several
drill holes, including SUU08005 and SUU08008B have confirmed an inferred
resource.&#160; SUU08005 intercepted the
Central lens at Suuri at a depth of approximately 1,000 metres and returned 4.0
g/t gold over 13.1 metres (including a 5.3 m interval grading 6.4 g/t).&#160; Hole SUU08008B cut a similar thick interval
of mineralization associated with the Central lens (2.8 g/t over 21.0 metres
including 4.1 g/t over a more narrow interval of 2.8 metres), but at a more
shallow depth over 200 metres away from SUU08005.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">One of the most
significant intercepts was in hole ETE08002 on Section&nbsp;36170N, which cut
the Western lens and returned 5.6 g/t gold over 3.5 metres in mineralization at
a depth of approximately 500 metres.&#160;
Although this intercept is not the deepest (about five intersections in
the Western lens are known at about 700 metres depth further North at Suuri),
it is significant because, prior to this intersection, the drilling had been so
widely spaced and continuity was not as certain.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Central Roura Zone May&nbsp;Be Strike Extension of Main Suuri Deposit
at Kittila</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Over 500 metres north of
the Suuri zone intercepts, deep drilling of the Central Roura zone has
continued to return significant results which may eventually lead to another
expansion of the deep gold resource at Kittila.&#160;
Hole ROU08002 cut 4.0 g/t gold over 6.1 metres at a depth of almost 750
metres.&#160; In 2009, four drills will test
Suuri and Roura at depth.&#160; A scoping
study is currently underway to investigate the economic potential of mining
these deep gold resources at Suuri and </font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">7</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Roura and expand gold
production at Kittila.&#160; The study is
expected to be complete in the fourth quarter of 2009.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

extensions to open pit and underground reserves at shallow depths of the
Kittila deposit, which is open to the north.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">The Kittila mine and the
surrounding Suurikuusikko property in Finland are beginning to show their
potential for the discovery of 5 million ounces or more of gold reserves,
similar to the LaRonde deposit and the entire Doyon-LaRonde gold trend in the
Abitibi.&#160; Consequently, the 2009
exploration budget for Kittila is the largest ever at approximately $16
million, and includes 67,500 metres in diamond drilling, with up to 8 drill
rigs operating throughout the year to help identify the gold reserve and
resource potential of the Kittila mine property.&#160; In addition, almost $5 million of exploration
expense, including an estimated 18,500 metres of diamond drilling, is planned
for exploration along the 25 kilometre Suurikuusikko gold trend and other
targets in Finland.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">About Agnico-Eagle</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in .3pt .0001pt 0in;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Agnico-Eagle
is a long established Canadian gold producer with operations located in Quebec
and Finland and exploration and development activities in Canada, Finland,
Mexico and the United States.&#160;
Agnico-Eagle&#146;s LaRonde mine is Canada&#146;s largest operating gold mine in
terms of reserves.&#160; The Company has full
exposure to higher gold prices consistent with its policy of no forward gold
sales.&#160; It has declared a cash dividend
for 27 consecutive years.&#160; </font><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Agnico-Eagle&#146;s
registered office is located at 145 King Street East, Suite&nbsp;400, Toronto,
Ontario M5C 2Y7.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8</font></p>

<div align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">the Company with respect to, among other
things, grade, tonnage, processing, mining methods, capital costs, total cash
costs, minesite costs, and location of surface infrastructure and actual
results and final decisions may be materially different from those current
anticipated.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Notes To Investors
Regarding The Use Of Resources</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cautionary Note To
Investors Concerning Estimates Of Measured And Indicated Resources.</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This press
release may use the terms &#147;measured resources&#148; and &#147;indicated resources&#148;. We
advise investors that while those terms are recognized and required by Canadian
regulations, the SEC does not recognize them. <b>Investors
are cautioned not to assume that any part or all of mineral deposits in these
categories will ever be converted into reserves</b>.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cautionary Note To
Investors Concerning Estimates Of Inferred Resources.</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This press
release may also use the term &#147;inferred resources&#148;. We advise investors that
while this term is recognized and required by Canadian regulations, the SEC
does not recognize it. &#147;Inferred resources&#148; have a great amount of uncertainty
as to their existence, and great uncertainty as to their economic and legal
feasibility. It cannot be assumed that all or any part of an inferred mineral
resource will ever be upgraded to a higher category. Under Canadian rules,
estimates of inferred mineral resources may not form the basis of feasibility
or pre-feasibility studies, except in rare cases. <b>Investors are cautioned not to assume that part or all of an inferred
resource exists, or is economically or legally mineable.</b></font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Scientific And Technical
Data</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Agnico-Eagle
Mines Limited is reporting mineral resource and reserve estimates in accordance
with the CIM guidelines for the estimation, classification and reporting of
resources and reserves.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cautionary Note To U.S.
Investors</font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">  <b>-</b> The
SEC permits U.S. mining companies, in their filings with the SEC, to disclose
only those mineral deposits that a company can economically and legally extract
or produce. We use certain terms in this press release, such as &#147;measured&#148;, &#147;indicated&#148;,
and &#147;inferred&#148;, and &#147;resources&#148; that the SEC guidelines strictly prohibit U.S.
registered companies from including in their filings with the SEC. U.S.
Investors are urged to consider closely the disclosure in our Form&nbsp;20-F,
which may be obtained from us, or from the SEC&#146;s website at: </font><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">http://idea.sec.gov.&#160; A &#147;final&#148;
or &#147;bankable&#148; feasibility study is required to meet the requirements to
designate reserves under Industry Guide 7.&#160;
Estimates were calculated using historic three-year average metals
prices and foreign exchange rates in accordance with the SEC Industry Guide
7.&#160; Industry Guide 7 requires the use of
prices that reflect current economic conditions at the time of reserve
determination which Staff of the SEC has interpreted to mean historic
three-year average prices.&#160; The assumptions
used for the mineral reserves and resources estimate reported by the Company on
February&nbsp;18th, 2009 were based on three year&#160; average prices for the period ending December&nbsp;31,
2008&#160; of $725 per ounce&#160; gold, $13.32 per ounce silver, $1.27 per
pound zinc, $3.15 per pound copper, $0.90 per pound lead and C$/US$, US$/Euro
and MXP/US$ exchange rates of 1.09, 1.37 and 11.00, respectively.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Canadian
Securities Administrators&#146; National Instrument 43-101 (&#147;NI 43-101&#148;) requires
mining companies to disclose reserves and resources using the subcategories of &#147;proven&#148;
</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">12</font></p>

<div align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='12',FILE='C:\JMS\105566\09-6875-1\task3403982\6875-1-ka-05.htm',USER='105566',CD='Mar  4 21:49 2009' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">reserves, &#147;probable&#148;
reserves, &#147;measured&#148; resources, &#147;indicated&#148; resources and &#147;inferred&#148; resources.
Mineral resources that are not mineral reserves do not have demonstrated
economic viability.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A mineral
reserve is the economically mineable part of a measured or indicated resource
demonstrated by at least a preliminary feasibility study. This study must
include adequate information on mining, processing, metallurgical, economic and
other relevant factors that demonstrate, at the time of reporting, that
economic extraction can be justified. A mineral reserve includes diluting
materials and allows for losses that may occur when the material is mined. A
proven mineral reserve is the economically mineable part of a measured resource
for which quantity, grade or quality, densities, shape and physical
characteristics are so well established that they can be estimated with
confidence sufficient to allow the appropriate application of technical and
economic parameters, to support production planning and evaluation of the
economic viability of the deposit. A probable mineral reserve is the
economically mineable part of an indicated mineral resource for which quantity,
grade or quality, densities, shape and physical characteristics can be
estimated with a level of confidence sufficient to allow the appropriate
application of technical and economic parameters, to support mine planning and
evaluation of the economic viability of the deposit.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A mineral
resource is a concentration or occurrence of natural, solid, inorganic or
fossilized organic material in or on the earth&#146;s crust in such form and
quantity and of such a grade or quality that it has reasonable prospects for
economic extraction. The location, quantity, grade, geological characteristics
and continuity of a mineral resource are known, estimated or interpreted from
specific geological evidence and knowledge. A measured mineral resource is that
part of a mineral resource for which quantity, grade or quality, densities,
shape, physical characteristics, can be estimated with a level of confidence
sufficient to allow the appropriate application of technical and economic
parameters, to support mine planning and evaluation of the economic viability of
the deposit. The estimate is based on detailed and reliable exploration,
sampling and testing information gathered through appropriate techniques from
locations such as outcrops, trenches, pits, workings and drill holes that are
spaced closely enough to confirm both geological and grade continuity. An
indicated mineral resource is that part of a mineral resource for which
quantity, grade or quality, densities, shape and physical characteristics can
be estimated with a level of confidence sufficient to allow the appropriate
application of technical and economic parameters, to support mine planning and
evaluation of the economic viability of the deposit. The estimate is based on
detailed and reliable exploration and testing information gathered through appropriate
techniques from locations such as outcrops, trenches, pits, workings and drill
holes that are spaced closely enough for geological and grade continuity to be
reasonable assumed. An inferred mineral resource is that part of a mineral
resource for which quantity and grade or quality can be estimated on the basis
of geological evidence and limited sampling and reasonably assumed, but not
verified, geological and grade continuity. The estimate is based on limited
information and sampling gathered through appropriate techniques from locations
such as outcrops, trenches, pits, workings and drill holes.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The mineral
reserves presented in this disclosure are exclusive of mineral resources.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The contents of
this press release have been prepared under the supervision of, and reviewed
by, Marc Legault P.Eng., Vice-President Project Development and a &#147;Qualified
Person&#148; for the purposes of NI 43-101.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">13</font></p>

<div align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>
